function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.450!');

	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

	warn('Directory could not be created: dev/logo');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logo', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of dev/logo');
}

if (is_file('dev/logo/logo.psd') && (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo.psd') != '124e3e4f74ed65e4f399c98cc15c7603c285e48a')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logo/logo.psd');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logo/logo.psd');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logo/logo.psd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/logo/logo.psd', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/logo/logo.psd')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logo/logo.psd');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo.psd') != '124e3e4f74ed65e4f399c98cc15c7603c285e48a') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logo/logo.psd');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logo/logo.psd', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logo/logo.psd');
}

	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/ironbase/logo.png');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '3cb9efa2d7b14ed50abbcad50a52a45eb1301b14') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3cb9efa2d7b14ed50abbcad50a52a45eb1301b14') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '48769531d2a1e6ea69d0e2d6da1991f2121e4dc1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3cb9efa2d7b14ed50abbcad50a52a45eb1301b14') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '00e54c78461cd1eeb2afa4409df874fa02b420d2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '00e54c78461cd1eeb2afa4409df874fa02b420d2') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '27fe1d5740c5e9ff196cf594fee8f6399047e6e6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '00e54c78461cd1eeb2afa4409df874fa02b420d2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') != '1444d46e8aa68d691b6e3c4f22e49e50a9bbc989') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '1444d46e8aa68d691b6e3c4f22e49e50a9bbc989') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== 'e32d748cc549223bc1a52da2a060da9d4db1ac8d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '1444d46e8aa68d691b6e3c4f22e49e50a9bbc989') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') != '3b2520550c7d45ab36ce853fd04af99711153b3e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '3b2520550c7d45ab36ce853fd04af99711153b3e') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '949e2f4a813e80ca0b5fcc1d7ce80988d923a9ab') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '3b2520550c7d45ab36ce853fd04af99711153b3e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'ac6b4ab71d6f867c922c257b8d706e52edd07c3c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ac6b4ab71d6f867c922c257b8d706e52edd07c3c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'e2583d2305282e2ea6342f045e7bbd88e0bc4c48') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ac6b4ab71d6f867c922c257b8d706e52edd07c3c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('userdata/styles/info.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: userdata/styles/info.txt');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('userdata/styles/info.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/styles/info.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') != '61e30b64da1e5dbe15a46eb6e0c5a864363a8b29') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/styles/info.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/styles/info.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/styles/info.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') !== '61e30b64da1e5dbe15a46eb6e0c5a864363a8b29') {
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') !== '70c00471d8c152323d7c66cdb70b114279e8abd0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/styles/info.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/styles/info.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/styles/info.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('userdata/styles/info.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/styles/info.txt') !== '61e30b64da1e5dbe15a46eb6e0c5a864363a8b29') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): userdata/styles/info.txt');
		}
	}
}
